		completion_reward = {
			unlock_decision_tooltip = {
				decision = form_hre
				show_effect_tooltip = no
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = ROOT
						ROOT = {
							has_wargoal_against = PREV
						}
					}
					OR = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_in_array = { HRE_states = THIS }
						}
						any_controlled_state = {
							is_in_array = { HRE_states = THIS }
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					clear_temp_array = temp_states
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { HRE_states = THIS }
							NOT = {
								is_in_array = { temp_states = THIS }
							}
						}
						add_to_temp_array = {
							temp_states = THIS
						}
					}
					every_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { HRE_states = THIS }
							NOT = {
								is_in_array = { temp_states = THIS }
							}
						}
						add_to_temp_array = {
							temp_states = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = take_state_focus
						target = PREV
						generator = temp_states
					}
				}
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_skip_one_line_tt

			add_relation_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = CZE_usurp_the_mantle
			}
		}
	}
